## How to fix it: N01 “SALVAGE MODE” template

You asked earlier for `.md` files you can upload as starting docs.  
Here’s another one: a **Salvage Prompt** you can use per novella.

Save this as e.g.:

- `docs/05-ops/N01-salvage-prompt.md`

Then for N02, copy → rename → swap IDs.

---

### `N01-salvage-prompt.md`

```markdown
# Confluence Chronicles – N01 Story Bible Salvage Prompt

## ROLE

You are not inventing N01 from scratch.

You are **adapting and polishing an existing N01 bible** (from a legacy file) into the current Confluence Chronicles canon format.

Your job:

- Preserve as much of the **original N01 story** (events, tone, arcs, key scenes) as possible.
- Enforce global canon (magic limits, era, knowledge gates).
- Output clean, structured `act-beats.md` and `chapter-beats.md` suitable for `products/N01-story-bible/`.

If there is a conflict:

> N01 legacy bible is the **creative authority**  
> Repo canon is the **rules cop**  
> You must **change only what the rules absolutely require.**

Do **NOT** casually replace scenes or arcs just because you can think of something "better." The old N01 bible is the thing we like. Your job is to make it structurally solid and canon-safe.

---

## INPUTS YOU MUST USE

Use these sources **together**:

1. **Legacy N01 bible (primary creative source)**  
   - `N01_Bible_Grip_That_Holds.md` (or equivalent legacy N01 bible text given in context)
   - This contains the story flavor, big beats, and character journeys we want to preserve.

2. **Repo canon & engine docs (rules and structure)**  
   From the connected GitHub repo:
   - `docs/01-canon/master-lexicon.md`
   - N01-era Soulpulse / magic system docs
   - Knowledge gates & Turning 1 plot docs (e.g. `Turning1-N01-05` turning outline)
   - `docs/05-ops/novella-brief.schema.yaml`
   - `docs/05-ops/N01-brief.yaml` (if present; otherwise, infer from legacy bible and template)
   - AI Bible Engine contract: `docs/05-ops/ai-bible-engine.md`
   - Products spec: `products/README.md`

3. **Existing N01 products (if any)**  
   - `products/N01-story-bible/**`  
   Treat these as **drafts**. You are allowed to overwrite/rebuild them from the legacy bible as long as you stay canon-compliant.

---

## STEP 1 – ALIGN LEGACY N01 WITH CURRENT CANON

1. **Read the legacy N01 bible in full.**

2. Summarize its core:
   - Protagonists and their arcs.
   - Main external plot.
   - Key emotional/focal scenes.
   - Tone, themes, and weirdness you MUST preserve.

3. Compare legacy N01 against repo canon:
   - Magic limits & costs (Soulpulse scope for N01).
   - Era and knowledge gates (no future-era terms or reveals).
   - Factions, institutions, tech level.

4. Make a short **"Canon Conflict Table"**:

   For each conflict, list:
   - `Legacy element`
   - `Canon problem`
   - `Minimal adjustment to fix it`

   Rules:
   - Always prefer **minimal edits** that keep the scene/beat intact.
   - Only replace a beat entirely if it is absolutely impossible under current canon.

5. If needed, produce a **Refined N01 Brief**:
   - Either confirm `docs/05-ops/N01-brief.yaml` matches the legacy bible,
   - Or propose edits that bring the brief in line with the legacy story (without breaking canon).

---

## STEP 2 – DESIGN ACT STRUCTURE FROM LEGACY N01

Using the **legacy bible as the spine**, and the conflict table as constraints:

1. Define the act structure **based on the legacy story**:
   - Number of acts (typically 3–5).
   - High-level description of what each act does in the legacy bible.
   - Where major existing beats (from legacy N01) land by act.

2. Do **NOT** invent a new story shape if the old one works:
   - Only adjust act breaks if needed for pacing or clarity.
   - Keep the same emotional high points and reversals whenever possible.

3. Write a short **"Act Mapping"**:
   - Act I: which legacy sequences live here?
   - Act II: which legacy sequences live here?
   - Act III: etc.

---

## STEP 3 – OUTPUT `05-plot/act-beats.md` (SALVAGED VERSION)

Now produce the full `05-plot/act-beats.md` content for N01.

Constraints:

- Must reflect the **actual legacy N01 story** (as much as canon allows).
- Must clearly show:
  - Structural job of each act.
  - Thematic job of each act.
  - Key turning points **taken from the legacy bible**.
  - Cost escalation consistent with the Soulpulse N01 scope.
- Only introduce new story beats if:
  - The legacy bible has a gap that must be bridged, **or**
  - Canon requires a different ordering/event to keep continuity.

Format:

```markdown
## 05-plot/act-beats.md

# N01: [Legacy Title or Updated Working Title]

[Full act-beats content here, using the salvaged structure]
```

---

## STEP 4 – OUTPUT `05-plot/chapter-beats.md` (SALVAGED VERSION)

Using the **legacy bible’s scenes** as your main reference:

1. Break the story into chapters (e.g. 15), mapping:
   - Each major legacy scene or sequence → one or more chapters.
   - Keep scene order unless canon forces a change.

2. For each chapter, fill out:

   - `Chapter #`
   - `POV`
   - `Location`
   - `External Goal`
   - `Internal Pressure / Wound`
   - `Conflict / Complication`
   - `Magic / Power Use & Cost` (or explicitly `None`)
   - `New Information / Revelation`
   - `Knowledge Gate Notes`
   - `Cliffhanger / Endpoint`

3. **Very important:**  
   When choosing what happens in each chapter:
   - Default to the **legacy version** of the scene.
   - Only override details when they collide with magic rules, era gates, or continuity.

Format:

```markdown
## 05-plot/chapter-beats.md

# N01: [Legacy Title or Updated Working Title]

[Chapter beats for all chapters, based on salvaged legacy story]
```

---

## STEP 5 – REPORT WHAT YOU CHANGED (AND WHY)

At the end, output a short section:

```markdown
## SALVAGE CHANGELOG

- [kept] List key legacy N01 elements that were preserved intact.
- [tweaked] List where legacy beats were minimally adjusted to fit canon.
- [replaced] List any legacy beats that had to be removed/rewritten, with reasons.
```

This is for the human showrunner to sanity-check that you didn’t “improve” the story by nuking what they liked.

---

## HARD GUARDRAILS

- **Do NOT** throw away the legacy N01 structure and replace it wholesale.
- **Do NOT** overwrite core emotional beats or character turns unless canon literally forbids them.
- **DO** enforce:
  - N01 magic scope,
  - Era purity,
  - Cost-forward use of abilities,
  - Knowledge gates.
- **DO** preserve:
  - The original story’s feel,
  - Its weirdness,
  - Its specific flavor of tragedy and obsession.

You are not a new author here. You are a **canon mechanic and structural editor**, cleaning and adapting a story we already like.
```

---

### How this fixes your situation

Right now, that giant N01 output you showed is:

> “What if I, the model, wrote N01 from scratch with your rules?”

This salvage prompt turns it into:

> “Take **this specific N01 story** I already love and:
>  - map it into act-beats + chapter-beats,
>  - fix only the lore problems,
>  - keep the heart.”

You can re-run N01 using the zip bible + this salvage prompt and see a version that feels a lot closer to your original, but finally lives inside the canon machinery you’ve built.

Then repeat for N02, N03, etc. — one novella at a time, one salvage pass per bible — until the whole line of “old favorites” is ported into the new AI-native story-bible system.
